25 Rest angle
-ve movement when ++angle  ^wMjYmcY8

Rest angle 
 ^EXl1J8FH

It is the angle of the servo when the robot is normally standing ^Ncz6sF1V

If Rest angle is 0 or 180 , if we keep increasing/decrease the angle the moton will be only on one side and the rest position will consume any energy as the motors rest position and the center of mass will be parallel to the gravity  ^KVb5ZCUv

+Ve movement ^fPoJaxn6

-ve movement ^sfOhYluw

Movement ^CGRRxN8Q

-ve Movement is in the sense that when the angle is increasing the motor will move opposite to the motion showed in the picture ^HprvxWAR

Lateral Rise when ++angle ^D2I30lbs
